    WHERE [r0].[Activo] = CAST(1 AS bit) AND [o].[Activo] = CAST(1 AS bit)
) AS [t] ON [r].[IdRol] = [t].[IdRol]
WHERE [u].[UsuarioId] = @__userId_0
ORDER BY [u].[IdUsuarioSistema], [s].[IdSistema], [r].[IdRol], [t].[Orden], [t].[IdRolObjeto]
